    // (undocumented)

    // (undocumented)
    status: "500";
}

    // (undocumented)

}

    packageConnectionManagers?: Record<string, Record<string, SsisExecutionParameterOutput>>;
    packageLocation: SsisPackageLocationOutput;
    packageParameters?: Record<string, SsisExecutionParameterOutput>;
    projectConnectionManagers?: Record<string, Record<string, SsisExecutionParameterOutput>>;
    projectParameters?: Record<string, SsisExecutionParameterOutput>;
    propertyOverrides?: Record<string, SsisPropertyOverrideOutput>;
    runtime?: any;
}

    flush(libraryName: string, options?: LibraryFlushParameters): Promise<LibraryFlush200Response | LibraryFlush202Response | LibraryFlushdefaultResponse>;
    get(libraryName: string, options?: LibraryGetParameters): Promise<LibraryGet200Response | LibraryGet304Response | LibraryGetdefaultResponse>;
    getOperationResult(operationId: string, options?: LibraryGetOperationResultParameters): Promise<LibraryGetOperationResult200Response | LibraryGetOperationResult202Response | LibraryGetOperationResultdefaultResponse>;
    list(options?: LibraryListParameters): Promise<LibraryList200Response | LibraryListdefaultResponse>;
}

// @public
export function paginate<TResponse extends PathUncheckedResponse>(client: Client, initialResponse: TResponse, options?: PagingOptions<TResponse>): PagedAsyncIterableIterator<PaginateReturn<TResponse>>;

// @public
export type PaginateReturn<TResult> = TResult extends {
    body: {
        value?: infer TPage;
    };
} ? GetArrayType<TPage> : Array<unknown>;

// @public
export interface PagingOptions<TResponse> {
    customGetPage?: GetPage<PaginateReturn<TResponse>[]>;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface ParameterSpecification {
    defaultValue?: any;
    type: "Object" | "String" | "Int" | "Float" | "Bool" | "Array" | "SecureString";
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface ParameterSpecificationOutput {
    defaultValue?: any;
    type: "Object" | "String" | "Int" | "Float" | "Bool" | "Array" | "SecureString";
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface Routes {
    (path: "/kqlScripts"): KqlScriptsGetAll;
    (path: "/kqlScripts/{kqlScriptName}", kqlScriptName: string): KqlScriptCreateOrUpdate;
    (path: "/kqlScripts/{kqlScriptName}/rename", kqlScriptName: string): KqlScriptRename;
    (path: "/metastore/create-database-operations/{id}", id: string): MetastoreRegister;
    (path: "/metastore/update-database-operations/{id}", id: string): MetastoreUpdate;
    (path: "/metastore/databases/{id}", id: string): MetastoreDelete;
    (path: "/sparkconfigurations"): SparkConfigurationGetSparkConfigurationsByWorkspace;
    (path: "/sparkconfigurations/{sparkConfigurationName}", sparkConfigurationName: string): SparkConfigurationCreateOrUpdateSparkConfiguration;
    (path: "/sparkconfigurations/{sparkConfigurationName}/rename", sparkConfigurationName: string): SparkConfigurationRenameSparkConfiguration;
    (path: "/bigDataPools"): BigDataPoolsList;
    (path: "/bigDataPools/{bigDataPoolName}", bigDataPoolName: string): BigDataPoolsGet;
    (path: "/dataflows/{dataFlowName}", dataFlowName: string): DataFlowCreateOrUpdateDataFlow;
    (path: "/dataflows/{dataFlowName}/rename", dataFlowName: string): DataFlowRenameDataFlow;
    (path: "/dataflows"): DataFlowGetDataFlowsByWorkspace;
    (path: "/createDataFlowDebugSession"): DataFlowDebugSessionCreateDataFlowDebugSession;
    (path: "/queryDataFlowDebugSessions"): DataFlowDebugSessionQueryDataFlowDebugSessionsByWorkspace;
    (path: "/addDataFlowToDebugSession"): DataFlowDebugSessionAddDataFlow;
    (path: "/deleteDataFlowDebugSession"): DataFlowDebugSessionDeleteDataFlowDebugSession;
    (path: "/executeDataFlowDebugCommand"): DataFlowDebugSessionExecuteCommand;
    (path: "/datasets"): DatasetGetDatasetsByWorkspace;
    (path: "/datasets/{datasetName}", datasetName: string): DatasetCreateOrUpdateDataset;
    (path: "/datasets/{datasetName}/rename", datasetName: string): DatasetRenameDataset;
    (path: "/getGitHubAccessToken"): WorkspaceGitRepoManagementGetGitHubAccessToken;
    (path: "/integrationRuntimes"): IntegrationRuntimesList;
    (path: "/integrationRuntimes/{integrationRuntimeName}", integrationRuntimeName: string): IntegrationRuntimesGet;
    (path: "/libraries"): LibraryList;
    (path: "/libraries/{libraryName}/flush", libraryName: string): LibraryFlush;
    (path: "/libraryOperationResults/{operationId}", operationId: string): LibraryGetOperationResult;
    (path: "/libraries/{libraryName}", libraryName: string): LibraryDelete;
    (path: "/linkedservices"): LinkedServiceGetLinkedServicesByWorkspace;
    (path: "/linkedservices/{linkedServiceName}", linkedServiceName: string): LinkedServiceCreateOrUpdateLinkedService;
    (path: "/linkedservices/{linkedServiceName}/rename", linkedServiceName: string): LinkedServiceRenameLinkedService;
    (path: "/notebooks"): NotebookGetNotebooksByWorkspace;
    (path: "/notebooksSummary"): NotebookGetNotebookSummaryByWorkSpace;
    (path: "/notebooks/{notebookName}", notebookName: string): NotebookCreateOrUpdateNotebook;
    (path: "/notebooks/{notebookName}/rename", notebookName: string): NotebookRenameNotebook;
    (path: "/notebookOperationResults/{operationId}", operationId: string): NotebookOperationResultGet;
    (path: "/pipelines"): PipelineGetPipelinesByWorkspace;
    (path: "/pipelines/{pipelineName}", pipelineName: string): PipelineCreateOrUpdatePipeline;
    (path: "/pipelines/{pipelineName}/rename", pipelineName: string): PipelineRenamePipeline;
    (path: "/pipelines/{pipelineName}/createRun", pipelineName: string): PipelineCreatePipelineRun;
    (path: "/queryPipelineRuns"): PipelineRunQueryPipelineRunsByWorkspace;
    (path: "/pipelineruns/{runId}", runId: string): PipelineRunGetPipelineRun;
    (path: "/pipelines/{pipelineName}/pipelineruns/{runId}/queryActivityruns", pipelineName: string, runId: string): PipelineRunQueryActivityRuns;
    (path: "/pipelineruns/{runId}/cancel", runId: string): PipelineRunCancelPipelineRun;
    (path: "/sparkJobDefinitions"): SparkJobDefinitionGetSparkJobDefinitionsByWorkspace;
    (path: "/sparkJobDefinitions/{sparkJobDefinitionName}", sparkJobDefinitionName: string): SparkJobDefinitionCreateOrUpdateSparkJobDefinition;
    (path: "/sparkJobDefinitions/{sparkJobDefinitionName}/execute", sparkJobDefinitionName: string): SparkJobDefinitionExecuteSparkJobDefinition;
    (path: "/sparkJobDefinitions/{sparkJobDefinitionName}/rename", sparkJobDefinitionName: string): SparkJobDefinitionRenameSparkJobDefinition;
    (path: "/debugSparkJobDefinition"): SparkJobDefinitionDebugSparkJobDefinition;
    (path: "/sqlPools"): SqlPoolsList;
    (path: "/sqlPools/{sqlPoolName}", sqlPoolName: string): SqlPoolsGet;
    (path: "/sqlScripts"): SqlScriptGetSqlScriptsByWorkspace;
    (path: "/sqlScripts/{sqlScriptName}", sqlScriptName: string): SqlScriptCreateOrUpdateSqlScript;
    (path: "/sqlScripts/{sqlScriptName}/rename", sqlScriptName: string): SqlScriptRenameSqlScript;
    (path: "/triggers"): TriggerGetTriggersByWorkspace;
    (path: "/triggers/{triggerName}", triggerName: string): TriggerCreateOrUpdateTrigger;
    (path: "/triggers/{triggerName}/subscribeToEvents", triggerName: string): TriggerSubscribeTriggerToEvents;
    (path: "/triggers/{triggerName}/getEventSubscriptionStatus", triggerName: string): TriggerGetEventSubscriptionStatus;
    (path: "/triggers/{triggerName}/unsubscribeFromEvents", triggerName: string): TriggerUnsubscribeTriggerFromEvents;
    (path: "/triggers/{triggerName}/start", triggerName: string): TriggerStartTrigger;
    (path: "/triggers/{triggerName}/stop", triggerName: string): TriggerStopTrigger;
    (path: "/triggers/{triggerName}/triggerRuns/{runId}/rerun", triggerName: string, runId: string): TriggerRunRerunTriggerInstance;
    (path: "/triggers/{triggerName}/triggerRuns/{runId}/cancel", triggerName: string, runId: string): TriggerRunCancelTriggerInstance;
    (path: "/queryTriggerRuns"): TriggerRunQueryTriggerRunsByWorkspace;
    (path: "/workspace"): WorkspaceGet;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface RunFilterParameters {
    continuationToken?: string;
    filters?: Array<RunQueryFilter>;
    lastUpdatedAfter: Date | string;
    lastUpdatedBefore: Date | string;
    orderBy?: Array<RunQueryOrderBy>;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface RunQueryFilter {
    operand: "PipelineName" | "Status" | "RunStart" | "RunEnd" | "ActivityName" | "ActivityRunStart" | "ActivityRunEnd" | "ActivityType" | "TriggerName" | "TriggerRunTimestamp" | "RunGroupId" | "LatestOnly";
    operator: "Equals" | "NotEquals" | "In" | "NotIn";
    values: Array<string>;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface RunQueryOrderBy {
    order: "ASC" | "DESC";
    orderBy: "RunStart" | "RunEnd" | "PipelineName" | "Status" | "ActivityName" | "ActivityRunStart" | "ActivityRunEnd" | "TriggerName" | "TriggerRunTimestamp";
}

    appId?: string;

    schedulerInfo?: SparkSchedulerOutput;
    sparkPoolName?: string;
    state?: "not_started" | "starting" | "idle" | "busy" | "shutting_down" | "error" | "dead" | "killed" | "success" | "running" | "recovering";
    submitterId?: string;
    submitterName?: string;
    tags?: Record<string, string>;
    workspaceName?: string;
}

    // (undocumented)

    killedAt?: string;
    notStartedAt?: string;
    recoveringAt?: string;
    runningAt?: string;
    startingAt?: string;
    successAt?: string;
}

// @public
export interface TriggerOperations {
    createOrUpdateTrigger(triggerName: string, options: TriggerCreateOrUpdateTriggerParameters): Promise<TriggerCreateOrUpdateTrigger200Response | TriggerCreateOrUpdateTrigger202Response | TriggerCreateOrUpdateTriggerdefaultResponse>;
    deleteTrigger(triggerName: string, options?: TriggerDeleteTriggerParameters): Promise<TriggerDeleteTrigger200Response | TriggerDeleteTrigger202Response | TriggerDeleteTrigger204Response | TriggerDeleteTriggerdefaultResponse>;
    getEventSubscriptionStatus(triggerName: string, options?: TriggerGetEventSubscriptionStatusParameters): Promise<TriggerGetEventSubscriptionStatus200Response | TriggerGetEventSubscriptionStatusdefaultResponse>;
    getTrigger(triggerName: string, options?: TriggerGetTriggerParameters): Promise<TriggerGetTrigger200Response | TriggerGetTrigger304Response | TriggerGetTriggerdefaultResponse>;
    getTriggersByWorkspace(options?: TriggerGetTriggersByWorkspaceParameters): Promise<TriggerGetTriggersByWorkspace200Response | TriggerGetTriggersByWorkspacedefaultResponse>;
    startTrigger(triggerName: string, options?: TriggerStartTriggerParameters): Promise<TriggerStartTrigger200Response | TriggerStartTriggerdefaultResponse>;
    stopTrigger(triggerName: string, options?: TriggerStopTriggerParameters): Promise<TriggerStopTrigger200Response | TriggerStopTriggerdefaultResponse>;
    subscribeTriggerToEvents(triggerName: string, options?: TriggerSubscribeTriggerToEventsParameters): Promise<TriggerSubscribeTriggerToEvents200Response | TriggerSubscribeTriggerToEvents202Response | TriggerSubscribeTriggerToEventsdefaultResponse>;
    unsubscribeTriggerFromEvents(triggerName: string, options?: TriggerUnsubscribeTriggerFromEventsParameters): Promise<TriggerUnsubscribeTriggerFromEvents200Response | TriggerUnsubscribeTriggerFromEvents202Response | TriggerUnsubscribeTriggerFromEventsdefaultResponse>;
}

export interface XmlReadSettings extends FormatReadSettingsBase {
    compressionProperties?: CompressionReadSettings;
    detectDataType?: any;
    namespacePrefixes?: any;
    namespaces?: any;
    // (undocumented)
    type: "XmlReadSettings";
    validationMode?: any;
}

    detectDataType?: any;

    namespaces?: any;
    // (undocumented)

    validationMode?: any;
}

}
